# 5 Tips For Landing Page Design in Crowdfunding - LaunchBoom

[Menu](#)
 [](https://www.launchboom.com)
[Talk  \
To Us](/expert)

[![Kickstarter Quickstart Guide Learn the basics of Kickstarter in 15 minutes.  ](https://no-cache.hubspot.com/cta/default/9067418/interactive-175707718819.png)](https://cta-service-cms2.hubspot.com/web-interactives/public/v1/track/redirect?encryptedPayload=AVxigLLqelXymAggPanxbvOt%2BC2qbypeDdJLvPZYXe7keCsxRHas%2BJRcM862oq6l2jsPlbP26wcKO8Xxtx7TID%2BN7%2Bp7byfsRjdGTdyjKi5bW0%2BuGdJuEBHUJ%2Faz7BiH3UcvlfFrTbBbKAG6y%2BfnXT6QH2xc%2FutrNB9ZtEqfAOYnN22RicFENlDavOZlx8Tr8aB%2Bx%2Bmm7O0sdpicbq4N&webInteractiveContentId=175707718819&portalId=9067418)

![5 tips to design a landing page feature image](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/5-tips-to-design-a-landing-page-feature-image-1024x576.jpg)

Landing pages are an essential piece of the pre-campaign puzzle. [Every time we test a product’s viability in the crowdfunding market,](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/launchboom-learning-timeline-of-a-testboom/)
 we use them to educate and nurture leads. For those who want to build the funnel themselves, it can be tough knowing how to start the landing page design process.

There’s a lot to consider when building a landing page, from colors to page alignment. We’ve designed thousands of these pages over the years. Over that time, we’ve learned how to give ourselves the best chance of making products resonate. Here are 5 simple tips on how to design a landing page for crowdfunding that converts.

### Table of Contents

1.  [Tip #1: Determine your goal](#heading1)
    
2.  [Tip #2: Develop a strategy](#heading2)
    
3.  [Tip #3: Design. Don’t decorate!](#heading3)
    
4.  [Tip #4: Mobile first](#heading4)
    
5.  [Tip #5: Keep it simple](#heading5)
    
6.  [Key Takeaways](#heading6)
    

Contents

*   [Tip #1: Determine your goal](#tip-1-determine-your-goal)
    
*   [Tip #2: Develop a strategy](#tip-2-develop-a-strategy)
    
*   [Tip #3: Design. Don’t decorate!](#tip-3-design-dont-decorate)
    
*   [Tip #4: Mobile first](#tip-4-mobile-first)
    
*   [Tip #5: Keep it simple](#tip-5-keep-it-simple)
    
*   [Key Takeaways](#key-takeaways)
    

Tip #1: Determine your goal
---------------------------

Every landing page should have a goal. Without one, you’ll be completely aimless. To understand your goal, you can start by asking yourself a few basic questions like:

*   What do I want this landing page to accomplish?
*   Who do I want to attract?
*   What do I want them to think?
*   How do I want them to feel?

The answers to these questions will serve as the foundation that will guide every decision you make when designing your landing page.

For example, let’s break down how we determined our goal for [Author Clock,](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/just-launched-author-clock-296741-in-24-hours/)
 a campaign that went on to raise $1.3 million dollars on Kickstarter.

![Author Clock landing page design tips](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Author-Clock-1024x823.jpg)

#### What did we want to accomplish?

Author Clock is a clock that tells time using literary quotes, which is a completely unique product. We knew we wanted to make viewers of the page excited and intrigued.

#### Who did we want to attract?

The target audience for us was people with an interest in reading and literature, but that can be limiting. We decided to open it up to a broader technology and hobbyist audience. One way this informed our design was we had to make sure to use quotes that were written by recognizable names like William Shakespeare and Arthur Conan Doyle.

#### What did we want them to think?

We wanted them to think they were seeing something extremely creative and “novel!” We needed to accentuate the product’s unique selling propositions (USPs) through our imagery and copy.

#### How did we want them to feel?

We wanted the creative nature of the product to inspire the audience to let their own creativity out. We placed major design emphasis on the feature that lets backers add their own quotes that aren’t already in the clock’s database.

Tip #2: Develop a strategy
--------------------------

By now you’re probably asking yourself “where is the part where we talk about fonts, and colors?” I promise it’s coming. We have to cover the “boring stuff” first because that’s how you build the blueprint for any design.

Let’s look at how to develop a strategy. Once you’ve defined your goal, you can start asking yourself more specific questions.

*   Am I targeting men or women?
*   In what age range?
*   What kind of lifestyle do they live?

These questions are very important because they ultimately help you choose your fonts, colors, imagery, etc. You can see how we were able to determine these design choices on the Author Clock landing page.

![Author Clock landing page](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Author-Clock-landing-page-1024x823.jpg)

For Author Clock’s strategy, our intention was to include women in our marketing as much as we could. Generally, crowdfunding is a male-saturated market, but we recognized that this product had a very gender-neutral appeal.

Our designers intentionally chose fonts that had a gender-neutral feel and colors like light browns and blues that appealed to both a male and female palet.

For imagery, we wanted to feature the clock in spaces that readers would be familiar with, such as on desks and bookshelves. All of these decisions turned into a strategy that allowed Author Clock to achieve [strong reservation rates](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/crowdfunding-campaign-projection-model/)
 throughout the pre-campaign testing phase.

**Bonus Strategy Tip:** When it comes to images with hands, we’ve found that it’s almost always best to use male hands to reduce the risk of alienating them. Product shots that feature female hands might suggest that a product is strictly feminine. However, data suggests that women are not turned off in the same way by product shots featuring male hands.

[![FREE DOWNLOAD Kickstarter Quickstart Guide Crowdfunding can feel really overwhelming. This guide makes it easy to understand. Plus, it can be read in less than 15 minutes!  ](https://no-cache.hubspot.com/cta/default/9067418/interactive-175537018221.png)](https://cta-service-cms2.hubspot.com/web-interactives/public/v1/track/redirect?encryptedPayload=AVxigLK3i%2FPYpiL8JrQ4FmR4CAofTrbrsXTadReZRVR93mrk%2BOAFhtExGJyHuQch%2BFQrCe7HOwz53W1QQtfyYUAMkLwEO%2Bh2DseqCPHU%2BvAzlY6ZBaudLbZ83lvdIeo8fP%2BfOC90ZMETc5hmU4OtirJ6PebVAK1Od87ibmju7JzeUqg%2Fyf%2FLchZFD%2B2dgZUTDhLHJiUo4%2BCB%2BTwo0Ooh&webInteractiveContentId=175537018221&portalId=9067418)

Tip #3: Design. Don’t decorate!
-------------------------------

When you design a landing page, you need to make sure that you’re not just decorating. What do I mean by that?

Here’s how we define the difference: **design contributes value and works in favor of the goal while decoration is simply filler.** You might be questioning whether you’ll be able to tell the difference. Well, it’s actually simpler than you think.

As you’re revising your page ask yourself, “if I remove this element, would the design still be as effective?” If the answer is yes, then it’s decoration. If the answer is no, then it’s a crucial part of your design.

When you’re designing, you’re going to have to make a lot of decisions both big and small. Just remember that every decision you make should serve your original goal of the landing page.

For example, you’ll notice in the screenshots of our Author Clock landing page that the design is relatively simple. Nothing jumps off the page except for the product, and none of the sections are overdone. That was intentional.

It’s always better to pare down pages and get rid of fluff so that you can focus on correcting design based on user experience. One pain point with Author Clock was that people doubted the clock’s ability to tell obscure times like 4:53 with literary quotes.

Instead of trying to double down on something else like [prettier photography or more eye-popping visuals,](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/meet-the-team-creative-producers/)
 we addressed the issue with a simple gif that cycled through with random times in its database. This kind of design mindset is how you can consistently achieve better metrics.

Tip #4: Mobile first
--------------------

For every page you design, you’ll naturally design a version for desktop. But, more importantly, you’ll also be designing a version for mobile. Yes, desktop matters, but get used to this mantra: “mobile first.”

[Funnels for crowdfunding lead generation](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/how-to-build-a-lead-gen-funnel-for-kickstarter-or-indiegogo-that-converts/)
 usually start with a Facebook or Instagram ad. Viewers who see these ads are enticed into clicking on them to learn more about the product. That brings them right to your landing page.

On which kind of device do you think most people are viewing Facebook and Instagram ads? That’s right–mobile! **These days, more than 90% of the traffic that we get to our landing pages comes from mobile devices.**

Now that I’ve convinced you about the importance of designing for mobile, here’s a checklist we use to make sure our pages stay optimized:

1.  The Call to Action is clear
2.  Type is big enough for easy readability
3.  Type is dark enough for easy readability
4.  Images, GIFs, and videos are compressed so that they load faster
5.  No more than 2 fonts used
6.  Headlines are easily distinguishable
7.  If you want something clickable, make it obvious
8.  Balance spacing to reduce the amount of scroll

Tip #5: Keep it simple
----------------------

One of the quickest ways to get stuck during landing page design is to constantly think of it as a whole. It’s important to always keep your original goal in mind, but the overall layout can easily overwhelm you.

An easy way to avoid this is to break it down by sections. In the LaunchBoom formula, each section has a headline, a few lines of copy, and an image.

![Landing page design tips comparison chart](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Comparison-chart-1024x823.jpg)

When you finish one section, it’s on to the next one! This also gives you the chance to try out some design choices on a section-by-section basis. Once you’re happy with the results of one section, you can apply that design to the rest.

While design is fun, [it comes with a lot of responsibility.](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/meet-the-team-designers/)
 We have to create something that is fundamentally easy for users to navigate. The last thing you want is for a viewer to bounce because the user experience was bad. It’s much easier to tweak messaging to improve conversion rates rather than having to redo intricate design elements.

Many people are tempted to push their websites to crazy limits in order to stand out. **While we encourage innovation, remember to let your product be the example of that innovation.** The more familiar and simple your design is, the more comfortable and effective your page will be.

Key Takeaways
-------------

I hope you found this advice helpful. There’s a lot that goes into designing a landing page for crowdfunding that converts, but in summary:

*   Always start with defining your goal. This will be the roadmap for your entire design.
*   Know your target audience before choosing fonts and colors. Don’t just pick based on personal preference.
*   If something can be removed without negatively impacting the value of the page, you can remove it.
*   More than 90% of landing page traffic comes from mobile, so optimize your page for them.
*   Keep it simple!

* * *

Thank you for checking out our 5 tips for helping you create a landing page for your product. We’ve got a ton more great insights and an extremely talented crowdfunding team. If you’re interested in working with us to make sure your Kickstarter or Indiegogo campaign is the best it can be, [schedule a meeting with us today!](https://www.launchboom.com/apply/)

#### Bubba was a baggage handler at Jackson Hole Airport…

And no stranger to the frigid Wyoming winter temperature.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/1.jpg "LaunchBoom Home – 4.0 Update – Home page Redesign (July 2024)")

He created a product called the 4-Season Gloves that would change the game for outdoor enthusiasts. But with so much on the line, he wanted to make sure he did the launch right. So he used our system and was able to raise $270K – forever changing his life.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/2.jpg "LaunchBoom Home – 4.0 Update – Home page Redesign (July 2024)")

Since then, we’ve helped him launch two more products, bringing the total amount raised to $1,814,602. And today, Bubba has his dream job: running his multi-million dollar brand called Give’r.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/3.jpg "LaunchBoom Home – 4.0 Update – Home page Redesign (July 2024)")

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/launchboom-testimonial-2.jpg "LaunchBoom Home – 4.0 Update – Home page Redesign (July 2024)")

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/stars.svg) on Google

"The combination of energy, creativity, depth and hunger exhibited by the Team at Launchboom is both rare and inspiring. We are grateful for the opportunity to work alongside such talent and are proud to call them partners on our journey as a crowdfunded company. Just be sure you're ready to give 100%...and don't forget to buckle up!"

#### The Legends of Avantris team were just friends hanging out…

They loved to play and create D&D content. After six years, they had built up a big social following and were making some money

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/4.jpg "LaunchBoom Home – 4.0 Update – Home page Redesign (July 2024)")

But they knew they could turn their hobby into something so much more. So they went to work on their own product called The Crooked Moon, a folk horror D&D supplement.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/6.jpg "LaunchBoom Home – 4.0 Update – Home page Redesign (July 2024)")

And after working with us to help them launch it, their project became the most funded 5E D&D supplement in Kickstarter history, raising $4,020,234. Since the launch, the crew has been able to turn their passion project into their full-time project.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/5.jpg "LaunchBoom Home – 4.0 Update – Home page Redesign (July 2024)")

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/launchboom-testimonial-1.jpg "LaunchBoom Home – 4.0 Update – Home page Redesign (July 2024)")

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/stars.svg) on

"When we first decided to launch a Kickstarter campaign to build out a game publishing wing of our company, we already had a clear vision and a large, passionate audience. However, we were ignorant on the actual steps to successfully run a campaign. LaunchBoom proved to be the final missing piece and solved that problem for us."

#### Audrey came to us with a failed Kickstarter campaign…

When she launched her product Kublet on Kickstarter, she struggled to get traction.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/kickstarter-audrey.jpg "LaunchBoom Home – 4.0 Update – Home page Redesign (July 2024)")

So she ended up canceling the campaign and then immediately joined LaunchBoom. We helped her re-position her product & build a highly engaged pre-launch email list.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/canceled-launchboom.jpg "LaunchBoom Home – 4.0 Update – Home page Redesign (July 2024)")

The result? She relaunched Kublet and raised $150,210 in 30 days – giving her the funds she needed to focus on building her business.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/9.jpg "LaunchBoom Home – 4.0 Update – Home page Redesign (July 2024)")

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/launchboom-review.jpg "LaunchBoom Home – 4.0 Update – Home page Redesign (July 2024)")

"We first did our campaign without LaunchBoom and raised $25k. After canceling the campaign and bringing LaunchBoom on board our relaunch raised $50k on the first day and eventually $150k. We could not have done this without the support of the amazing team at LaunchBoom."

One last thing...
-----------------

Hey – I’m Mark, CEO here at LaunchBoom.  
  
So sometimes my friends call me crazy. Because for the past 10 years I’ve been a _little_ obsessed with one thing... crowdfunding.  
  
Why?  
  
Well, let me tell you a quick story.  
  
Back in 2013 a few friends and I had a digital marketing agency – actually “agency” might be a bit of a stretch, we were more like a bunch of freelancers working from a garage (yes, for some reason we actually did that).  
  
But back to the story.  
  
We had another friend named Kevin who had an idea for a product called EcoQube.  
  
“Can you help me launch it on Kickstarter?” He asked.  
  
Now, I’ll admit – outside of hearing of Kickstarter before, we knew next to nothing about it. So how do blindly optimistic 20-something year olds answer?  
  
Well, “yes” of course.  
  
For months, we put everything we had into the campaign until finally, we were ready to launch.  
  
I still remember the feeling… excitement, anxiety and maybe a little bit of terror – all mixed into one.  
  
But nothing would prepare us for what happened next.  
  
The campaign raised $79,026. Kevin’s life was changed. And we were hooked.  
  
Crowdfunding allowed Kevin to not only launch his crazy idea, but _transform_ it into a business that he could focus on full-time. We hadn’t seen anything like it. And we wanted to do more.  
  
Well, with LaunchBoom, we've been able to do a lot more, working with thousands of product creators across the world.  
  
And we love it.  
  
This is our dream job. And we want to help you create yours. So no matter where you’re at with your product idea right now, we’re here to help.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/signature.svg)

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/Mark-Pecota-Headshot.jpeg)

Mark Pecota  
CEO of LaunchBoom  
Author of Crowdfunded

To Us](/expert)

Want free crowdfunding content?  
You're in the right place
-----------------------------------------------------------

Since the beginning of LaunchBoom, we’ve always focused on creating really good (and free) educational content. We want you to say “I can’t believe they’re giving this away!” when you dive into our stuff.

Why?

Well, it’s simple really. We believe you get back what you give – which is why we give super valuable content away for free knowing that the good karma will probably make its way back to us in the future.

So whether you work with us, someone else, or blaze your own trail with your campaign, feel free to utilize any of the resources available on this page.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/section2-icon.svg)

Learn 10 Years of Kickstarter  
Lessons in 45 Minutes
-----------------------------------------------------

You'll probably spend 1,000+ hours launching your product – spend less than 1 to learn how to launch it right. Our CEO, Mark, will take you from complete beginner to understanding exactly what you must do to have a successful Kickstarter.

[Watch here](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=E3QRiwv6ZC4)

 [Your browser does not support the video tag.](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=E3QRiwv6ZC4)

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/section3-icon.svg)

Get Sent a Newsletter  
You’ll Actually Want To Read
----------------------------------------------------

“Oh, great another newsletter!” We get it, there’s a million newsletters out there that claim to be valuable but end up just spamming you with promotions or surface level content. We aim to do the opposite. Every LaunchBoom newsletter is short, to the point, and filled with stuff that will deepen your understanding of crowdfunding.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/section3-w.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/section3-m.png)

Get the #1 bestselling

“We’ve had the opportunity to partner with LaunchBoom for a consulting service for our crowdfunding campaign. Paul Dysinger raised $341,796 for Seedtime

on Trustpilot

### Best investment I ever made

LaunchBoom showed me how to successfully raise capital for my Indiegogo campaign. Their hands-on program is flawless. This was probably the best investment I ever did. There is a secret recipe for crowdfunding and these guys show you how it's done.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/1586664609735.jpeg "Talk To An Expert")

Youri Benoiston raised $1,219,668 for Oculis Lodge

on Trustpilot

### More than just a guide to Kickstarters

More than just a guide to Kickstarters! LaunchBoom is also a guide to marketing, product positioning, communication and even storytelling. My only regret is not working with LaunchBoom sooner. There are a billion little details that you have to align in order to launch a Kickstarter and LaunchBoom helps with all of them, both in static resources and in direct auditing. Super cool stuff, and I plan on using their strategies for product research, direct communication, vigorous testing and feature/story focus paradigms for every game I make.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/1634596657411.jpeg "Talk To An Expert")

AC Atienza raised $216,929 for One Hit Heroes

on Trustpilot

### Best in the game

Our company, William Painter Inc. has worked with LaunchBoom on 3 separate campaigns that have raised over $1,000,000. LaunchBoom is definitely the best in the industry. They truly understand the Kickstarter backer and have an incredible team. Over the past several campaigns it has been a real pleasure working with their team.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/1517681797718.jpeg "Talk To An Expert")

Matt DeCelles raised $1,425,326 for William Painter

on Trustpilot

### Would recommend!

Working with LaunchBoom was overall a great experience. This was my first Kickstarter, so I was very oblivious of how to run a campaign, and Launchboom acted as my consultant throughout the entire process. The lessons were thorough, the responses were fast, and I feel as if I have learned so much. Shoutout to Soren - he's the man!

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/1566974666546.jpeg "Talk To An Expert")

Aaron Radcliffe raised $373,464 for Fyro

on Trustpilot

### An Easy Win for Nearly Any Project

The team at Launch Boom is thoughtful, and willing to help in any way they can. The process works, and you'll learn a ton along the way, especially if you aren't familiar with advertising concepts.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/1680324317532.jpeg "Talk To An Expert")

Mike Boseak raised $653,495 for Last Light 2nd Edition

on Trustpilot

### Exceptional Support and Results with LaunchBoom

I recently wrapped up my fourth Kickstarter campaign, and it was my first time working with LaunchBoom. This campaign raised over 20 times more than my previous three campaigns combined. While I had a great product, it wouldn’t have been nearly as successful without LaunchBoom.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/1575355585832.jpeg "Talk To An Expert")

Scott Salzman raised $468,628 for Desk Nest

on Trustpilot

### Our experience with LaunchBoom has been…

Our experience with Launchboom has been excellent! The program and all the associated tools are very user-friendly and the communication with the team is super good. Without Launchboom, our first Kickstarter campaign would not have been a success.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/1720178347976.jpeg "Talk To An Expert")

Jarne Pol raised $176,207 for Matero Cookware

on Trustpilot

### A great resource that sets realistic expectations

Where LaunchBoom really shines is through the resources it provides. If you have little experience with crowdfunding and want to do a lot yourself, this is an ideal service. There are templates, guides, and walkthroughs, but be prepared to do a lot yourself. They tell you what a successful ad entails and advise who to market to but you are still in charge with creating your marketing content—a plus in my view.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/1569947958480.jpeg "Talk To An Expert")

Ross Bruggink raised $555,283 for Vicious Gardens

on Trustpilot

### A Must for Beginners

There is a lot that goes into putting together a crowdfunding campaign, and if you are starting from scratch, I would be hard-pressed to find a better place to direct you towards than LaunchBoom. It is very much akin to a top-notch crowdfunding bootcamp. This program will save you more than your initial investment by helping you navigate around pitfalls alone.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/pic4908055.jpeg "Talk To An Expert")

J. Scott Rumptz raised $64,807 for NEXUS

FAQs
----

Is there a cost to this?

No! Both the LaunchBoom and Kickstarter video modules are complete free.

What can I expect to learn?

This course will take you through the basics (and then some) on every part of having a successful Kickstarter campaign.

How is this different than signing up to work with LaunchBoom?

For this course, we focused on the most foundational content for launching a successful Kickstarter. When you work with us, the strategy not only gets a bit more advanced, but you get to work directly with our team to guide you through it.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/02/logos-learning-lab.svg)

# How LaunchBoom Works | Kickstarter & Indiegogo Marketing

   

[Menu](#)
 [](https://www.launchboom.com)
[Talk  \
To Us](/expert)

Let’s get you funded in minutes.
--------------------------------

#### How? By having a successful pre-launch.

The pre-launch is the marketing work that happens **BEFORE** you go live with your campaign – and if you do it right, you’ll hit your funding goal on day one (aka what we call a LaunchBoom).

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/like-these.svg)

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/1.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/2.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/3.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/4.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/5.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/6.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/1.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/2.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/3.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/4.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/5.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/6.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/1.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/2.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/3.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/4.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/5.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/6.png)

Consider us your pre-launch partners.
-------------------------------------

Knowing the right path to take for your pre-launch is 99% of the challenge. But you don’t have to worry about that. Since 2013 we’ve pioneered the pre-launch, guiding over 1,000 product creators through our pre-launch process.

With over 100 years of combined experience in crowdfunding, our expert team wants to help you hit your funding goal and beyond.

![LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/section2-w.png "LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy")![LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/team.png "LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy")

#### Whether you just have an idea…

Like Emilie, the creator of Droplet, who came to us with photorealistic renderings and went on to raise **$114,507** on Kickstarter.

![LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/section3-m.jpg "LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy")![LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/section3-w.jpg "LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy")

#### Or a fully functioning prototype…

Like Tyler from Polycade, who had a working prototype when he joined LaunchBoom and went on to raise **$1,658,958.**

![LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/section3b-m.jpg "LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy")![LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/section3b-w.jpg "LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy")

Follow a process trusted  
by over 1,000 creators
-------------------------------------------------

![Superfan Funnel Icon](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/1section4icon-w-m.svg)

#### 1 Build a Superfan Funnel

What's a Superfan Funnel? Think of it as a series of web pages that help you build an email list of Superfans (people who can't wait to buy your product!). We help you use our software, LaunchKit, to make yours in minutes instead of days.

![Audience Icon](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/2section4icon-w-m.svg)

#### 2 Identify an audience who loves your product

Imagine a room full of hundreds of thousands of people, credit cards in hand, looking for a product just like yours. They're out there and our seasoned experts help you find them and speak to them – giving you clarity on the right marketing materials to create and the exact ad budget you'll need to reach your goals.

![Advertising Icon](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/3section4icon-w-m.svg)

#### 3 Build an audience quickly and profitably with advertising

With the knowledge gained from step 2, it almost feels like cheating. We help you spend your budget only on the ads that are working best, keeping your costs low and your ROI high.

![Launch Icon](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/4section4icon-w-m.svg)

#### 4 Have a LaunchBoom

Today's the day. It’s time to launch this puppy. Typically, this is when creators feel fear and doubt, but you feel excited and confident. Click that launch button, email your pre-launch audience, and hit your funding goal in minutes.

![Launch Boom Icon](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/5section4icon-w-m.svg)

#### 5Enjoy the unique benefits of quick funding

Besides the immediate revenue, quick funding has some awesome perks. Shoot up in the rankings on Kickstarter and get free traffic from the platform. Because of this, LaunchBoom Creators see 20-40% of all their funding come from Kickstarter itself.

Alright, temperature check.
---------------------------

We know that was a lot of information, but remember we’re here to help!

Before your campaign starts heating up we recommend talking with one of our experts.  
Share where you’re at in your journey and we’ll show you what this process might look like for you.

[Talk to an expert to learn more](https://www.launchboom.com/expert/)

Rather walk through the process with us?

diving into our system in these two quick videos.

#### Whatever brought you here, we’re so glad you made it.

We started 10 years ago as  
a group of friends in college…
-----------------------------------------------------------

As blindly optimistic 20-year-olds, we had big aspirations to build a  
successful marketing agency, taking on nearly every project we could find.

![LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/7-m.png "LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy")![LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/7-w-1.png "LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy")

**But everything changed** when Kevin asked if we could help launch his first Kickstarter campaign.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/8-m.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/kevin2-1-copy-1.png)

#### It raised $79,026 and 1 year later we launched his next product, raising another $375,058.

We realized that  
crowdfunding might just be our thing
-------------------------------------------------------

flash forward to the present day and we have…

**A team of experts** to guide you through launching your products

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/9-m.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/9-w-1.png)

And bringing **your games to life.**

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/10-m.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/10-w-1.png)

**And a team that continues to design and build LaunchKit,** our custom launch software that helps creators have wildly successful campaigns.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/11-m.png) ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/11-w-2.png)

LaunchBoom is more than our team.  
It’s a community of over 1,000 product  
creators who now have their dream job.

FamilyAlbum
---------------------------

Shhhh, we’re not supposed to show this to you, but you seem cool enough.

Our family album is our internal Slack channel that serves as a digital  
scrapbook for all of our memories and since you’re about to work alongside  
our team, we thought it might be nice to know us a little bit better.

Let’s make this a co-op game
----------------------------

Come for the marketing expertise, stay for the community.

Trying to get a game off the ground by yourself can be a bit lonely at times. That’s why community has been built into LaunchBoom Games from day one – a place where 300+ game creators just like you come to hang out, get feedback, and support each other.

![LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/4-lb.jpg "LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy")![LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/w-3-1.png "LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy")

We help game creators  
turn fantasy into reality
-------------------------------------------------

Unless it’s a fantasy game of course - but in all seriousness, we love  
helping game creators turn their ideas into successful game businesses.

#### Zoey & Casey were a midwest couple with a wedding photography business…

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/1-1.jpg "LaunchBoom Games")

They loved board games and always dreamed of launching their own. So in between their work, they started working on one that paid homage to their love of the outdoors. It’d be called Bear Mountain Camping Adventure, and after many months of work, it was finally ready.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/2-1.jpg "LaunchBoom Games")

So they joined LaunchBoom and got to work on their Kickstarter, building a community of superfans before their launch. And when they finally launched, they raised $781,450 – allowing them to go all-in on building their new game studio, SweaterBear Games.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/3-1.jpg "LaunchBoom Games")

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/casey-launchboom.jpg "LaunchBoom Games")

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/stars.svg) on Trustpilot

“LaunchBoom is the best of the best when it comes to getting ready for a successful launch! This is our first Kickstarter campaign, and with 9 days left we’re sitting at $650,000 raised with 6,800+ backers! Their consultants and resources are incredible!”  
  
– Casey Mattes, Founder of SweaterBear Games

#### Leonie was laid off from her job…

So she took the opportunity to develop a game idea she had called Biome.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/5-5.jpg "LaunchBoom Games")

From 6AM to midnight, she was all in. Working on the cards, the actions, and everything in between. Her game was basically done, but she didn’t know how to launch.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/4-3.jpg "LaunchBoom Games")

So she joined LaunchBoom to help her launch it on Kickstarter, raising $400,240 by the end of her campaign. And today, she works full-time on building her game studio called Lioness Games.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/6-2.jpg "LaunchBoom Games")

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/2-–-1.jpg "LaunchBoom Games")

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/stars.svg) on Trustpilot

“…I’m so glad we chose LaunchBoom. 1. The LB program is very well executed. 2. The team is incredible. Victor and Maria went above and beyond to help me and I’m so grateful for their support 3. The community of fellow board game creators is amazing and made the whole experience so much better. 4. My board game funded on Kickstarter in 9 minutes. The fee is well worth it!”  
  
– Leonie Grundler, Founder of Lioness Games

#### Ridge had a dream to be the next Marvel…

Like Marvel has the franchises of Spider-man, X-men, and Iron Man, Ridge wanted to do the same.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/8-1.jpg "LaunchBoom Games")

So he created Rising Empire Studios with the first franchise to be called Alpha Clash. First, he launched a graphic novel to kick off the franchise but was looking to do a trading card game next.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/7-1.jpg "LaunchBoom Games")

So he joined LaunchBoom to help him launch it and raised $422,809. Since then, he’s launched two more campaigns and continues to build out the Alpha Clash universe.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/9-1.jpg "LaunchBoom Games")

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/alpha-clash-launchboom.jpg "LaunchBoom Games")

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/stars.svg) on Trustpilot

“LaunchBoom created a community and a resource that teaches what crowdfunding is and showcases strategies on how to execute a successful campaign.”  
  
– Ridge Kiley, CEO at Rising Empire Studios

FAQ
---

Do I need a prototype?

Nope! You can begin ad testing with renders or artwork before your prototype is complete. In fact, it’s better to start earlier in the process. With our system, you can get real-time feedback about your product from real customers or our community and improve as you go.

Our program is set on a per-launch basis, not a fixed timeline. If you need to revisit the drawing board for your prototype, you can always hit pause and start again later OR build your list slowly as you refine your product.

How much advertising budget do I need?

No creator spends the same amount on ads, and we won’t know how much you’ll need until you test. For our testing phase, you’ll only need to spend between $1,000 to $2,000.

That’s because we only advise you to continue spending on advertising when the metrics show a likely positive return on investment. We take a gradual, stair-step approach to minimize risk, as opposed to throwing thousands of dollars into ad spend and hoping it works.

By using YOUR data from the testing phase, we are able to give you a more personalized and accurate budget.

What is the timeline to launch?

However long it takes to build a big enough email list.

In the past decade of launching crowdfunding campaigns, we’ve found that a pre-launch should last at least 2 months to ensure the best results. A quick AND successful pre-launch (less than 2 months) is extremely uncommon unless you already have an audience.

Learn how much time you should spend in pre-launch [here](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/how-long-should-a-prelaunch-take-to-get-the-best-results-for-a-crowdfunding-campaign/)
.

What platform should I launch on?

It depends on each project. We know: that’s everyone’s least favorite answer. But really, it does. Whether it’s Kickstarter, Gamefound, or BackerKit, our team can help you decide which is the best platform for you.

Do I need to use the $1 deposit strategy?

Nope! We have a few different pre-launch strategies and we’ll help you choose one that’ll work best for your campaign.

---

# FAQs | LaunchBoom

[Menu](#)
 [](https://www.launchboom.com)
[Talk  \
To Us](/expert)

You have questions?  
  
We have answers.
=========================================

FAQ
---

Do I need a prototype?

Nope! You can begin ad testing with renders before your prototype is complete. In fact, it’s better to start earlier in the process. With our system, you can get real-time feedback about your product from real customers and improve as you go.

Our program is set on a per-launch basis, not a fixed timeline. If you need to revisit the drawing board for your prototype, you can always hit pause and start again later OR build your list slowly as you refine your product.

How much advertising budget do I need?

No creator spends the same amount on ads, and we won’t know how much you’ll need until you test. For our testing phase, you’ll only need to spend between $1,000 to $2,000.

That’s because we only advise you to continue spending on advertising when the metrics show a likely positive return on investment. We take a gradual, stair-step approach to minimize risk, as opposed to throwing thousands of dollars into ad spend and hoping it works.

By using YOUR data from the testing phase, we are able to give you a more personalized and accurate budget.

How much am I going to raise?

The LaunchBoom process will give you clarity on how much you are going to raise. By advertising in the pre-launch, we can predict your campaign result using your own data. This not only reduces your risk, but gives you confidence as to when you should launch.

What is needed to get started? What creatives are needed?

You’ll only need renders and/or basic photography of your product to get started. These shouldn’t be too expensive for you to get. In fact, many of our creators’ best performing images were shot using a smartphone. Today, in the age of TikTok and Instagram, organic content usually performs much better than something that’s overly polished and expensive.

What is the timeline to launch?

However long it takes to build a big enough email list.

In the past decade of launching crowdfunding campaigns, we’ve found that a pre-launch should last at least 2 months to ensure the best results. A quick AND successful pre-launch (less than 2 months) is extremely uncommon unless you already have an audience.

Learn how much time you should spend in pre-launch [here](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/how-long-should-a-prelaunch-take-to-get-the-best-results-for-a-crowdfunding-campaign/)
.

How much does it cost to work with LaunchBoom?

We have a few different options depending on your product category & level of support you’re looking for. We also have _very_ founder-friendly payment plans available. Just ask!

What’s the best way to get in touch with your team?

Fill out the form [here](https://www.launchboom.com/expert/)
 to get in touch with our team. It’s super easy and takes less than a minute.

For basic questions, you can reach us at [\[email protected\]](/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)

Can you work with other agencies like Jellop?

Yes, although we work best with agencies that have complementary services to ours. For example, we have worked on many campaigns with Jellop.

Can I pause if I have a delay?

Yes. Our program covers one product launch. We understand there may be unforeseen delays in product development, which is why we don’t have a time limit. We recommend that creators begin testing with us as soon as possible. If there are delays, you can pause and always resume when you’re ready.

What platform should I launch on?

It depends. We know: that’s everyone’s least favorite answer. But really, it does. Whether it’s Kickstarter, Indiegogo, Gamefound, or BackerKit, our team can help you decide which is the best platform for you.

Is LaunchBoom a course?

No. While you will learn a lot working with us, our team is heavily involved in your campaign on a day-to-day basis.

Run A/B Tests
-------------

Stuck between two versions for your landing page? Test it and let the data show you which is better. Powerful A/B testing is built right into LaunchKit so you can test to your heart’s content.

*   ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/section3.svg)Set up A/B tests in minutes
*   ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/section3.svg)Analyze the results in real time
*   ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/section3.svg)Choose the winning version & test again

![LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/11/lk-ab.png "LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy")

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/section3e-w-m.svg)

Use LaunchBoom AI
-----------------

Take an hours-long process and complete it in minutes. Staring at a blank page trying to write persuasive marketing copy is a thing of the past with LaunchBoom AI. Tell it about your product, click a button, and BOOM! It will generate all your ad and landing page copy for you.

*   ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/section3.svg)Give the AI your product information
*   ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/section3.svg)Generate all the copy on your landing page
*   ![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/section3.svg)Get multiple versions of ad copy in different styles

![LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/section3e-w-m.png "LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy")

Be in the Driver’s  
Seat of Your Launch
----------------------------------------

LaunchKit puts you- not a third party platform- in the driver’s seat of your campaign so you can build your funnel on your own domain. We integrate with your payment processing and email marketing software, so payments and communications always go directly to you.

The Proven  
Software for high ROI
----------------------------------

Don’t leave money on the table for your campaign. Take it from these creators who used LaunchKit to elevate their ROI and achieve record breaking campaign numbers.

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/11/lk-1.png)

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/11/ring-one.png)

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/11/lk-3.png)

![](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/11/lk-4.png)

FAQ
---

How much does  
LaunchKit cost?

LaunchKit is available only for LaunchBoom clients and is included in every program we have. You can chat with us [here](https://www.launchboom.com/expert/)
 to learn more.

What is a Reservation  
Funnel?

The Reservation Funnel is a strategy developed by LaunchBoom that helps you build an email lists of superfans (AKA... people that can't wait to buy your product). It works by offering people a special discount or benefit by putting down a $1 deposit.

Do I have to use the  
Reservation Funnel?

Nope! We have a few different pre-launch funnels you can choose from and we’ll help you choose one that’ll work best for your campaign.

What kind of analytics  
does LaunchKit offer?

LaunchKit provides analytics for both your pre-launch ads and live campaign ads. Right now, we support Meta (Facebook & Instagram) Ads, Google Analytics, and the ability to track any custom source.

How robust is it? How  
easy to use is it?

LaunchKit was made for new creators and veteran creators alike. It's powerful software (as you can see from all the successful launches!) but it was designed to be easy and intuitive to use.

About the Speaker
-----------------

Will Ford is an American Entrepreneur and Crowdfunding Expert who is passionate about bringing innovation to life.

Will is the President of LaunchBoom and has built this brand to be one of the most respected in the crowdfunding industry.

Since July 2015, LaunchBoom has managed more successful reward-based crowdfunding campaigns than any other agency in the world. LaunchBoom is currently a Certified Expert on Kickstarter and a Certified Expert on Indiegogo and has helped thousands of Entrepreneurs worldwide make their dreams a reality.

Will is a member of EO (Entrepreneur’s Organization) in San Diego and has dedicated his career to helping early stage startups and Entrepreneurs succeed.

# How LaunchBoom predicts how much your campaign will raise with surprising accuracy [video] - LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy

[Menu](#)
 [](https://www.launchboom.com)
[Talk  \
To Us](/expert)

![campaign projection model](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Blog-Post-003-–-1-1024x576.png)

One of the most common questions clients ask is, “How much money is my crowdfunding campaign going to raise?”

Unfortunately, we don’t have a crystal ball that can predict your exact raise amount. But we do have the next best thing!

Crowdfunding Campaign Projection Model
--------------------------------------

After years of trial and error in crowdfunding, we’ve created a Campaign Projection Model that predicts what a campaign will raise with surprising accuracy.

**It’s so reliable because it’s based on real conversion data that we’ve collected from [hundreds of crowdfunding campaigns](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/what-crowdfunding-experts-have-learned-over-5000-campaigns/)
 we’ve launched across multiple [product categories](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/10-green-tech-crowdfunding-projects-we-love/)
 and price points.**

We use it on every campaign we take on and now it’s available to you.

Watch the video below to get an inside look at how our Campaign Projection Model Works and see it in action on a live campaign. Here we go!

[https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Campaign-Projection-Model.mp4](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Campaign-Projection-Model.mp4)

In this video, you will learn:
------------------------------

*   How high price point products perform compared to low price point products
*   How to predict your Return on Ad Spend (ROAS)
*   How to predict total email revenue
*   How to predict total VIP revenue (deposits)
*   How to predict total campaign revenue
*   4 scenarios based on different conversion rates
*   How the Projection Model performed on a live campaign

Want to talk with a team member about our Campaign Projection Model or other crowdfunding services? Book a call [here](https://www.launchboom.com/apply/)
!

# Just Launched: Author Clock - $296,741 in 24 Hours! - LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy

[Menu](#)
 [](https://www.launchboom.com)
[Talk  \
To Us](/expert)

![Author Clock 24 Hour Raise](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Blog-Post-001-–-1.3-–-5-1024x576.png)

Author Clock is “A Novel Way to Tell Time.” It contains thousands of quotes from notable authors and displays passages from literature that tell you the exact time of day.

Author Clock raised $296,741 in it’s first 24 hours on Kickstarter, and in this article, we’re going to break down how we used the LaunchBoom System to blow past six figures on Launch Day.

Contents

*   [Step 1: Messaging & Positioning](#step-1-messaging-positioning)
    
*   [Step 2: Testing With Our Reservation Funnel](#step-2-testing-with-our-reservation-funnel)
    
*   [Step 3: Scaling Our Best Assets With Proprietary Audiences](#step-3-scaling-our-best-assets-with-proprietary-audiences)
    
*   [Step 4: Implementing Our Learnings Into a High-Performance Campaign Page](#step-4-implementing-our-learnings-into-a-high-performance-campaign-page)
    

Step 1: Messaging & Positioning
-------------------------------

The starting point for every project we work with is figuring out how we want to position the product to the market.

Our Strategy Team extensively researches competitors to pinpoint what really makes Author Clock unique. Through this research, **we came up with three main messaging angles that we wanted to test**:

1.  **Stay Inspired**: Having Author Clock around is a great reminder to be creative and read new books that you haven’t heard of before.
2.  **Conversation/Statement Piece**: Author Clock fits beautifully in any bookworm’s home, and is a unique decoration that’s sure to spark conversations from guests.
3.  **Join a Community**: Author Clock allows users to submit quotes to be displayed on the clock, allowing you to contribute and connect with a community of fellow book lovers.

After identifying what made Author Clock special, we focused on figuring out which audiences we wanted to target on Facebook.

Our Strategy Team decided on these four audiences:

*   Literature/Classic Authors
*   Kindle & Book Stores
*   Interior Design
*   Minimalism

We determined that these audiences would resonate the most with our messaging, and would be the best core users to [test our ads](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/how-to-make-ads-that-work/)
 and landing pages on before scaling out to larger audiences.

Step 2: Testing With Our Reservation Funnel
-------------------------------------------

Once we have our initial strategy developed, the next step is testing it through our custom Landing Page and Reservation Funnel to optimize our ad creative to get the best lead intent (measured by Cost per Lead) and purchase intent (measured by Cost per Reservation).

Here’s what our funnel looks like:

![LaunchBoom reservation funnel overview](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Funnel.jpg)

The ultimate goal of the reservation is to get the user to put down a $1 deposit to reserve the product before you launch. Why? [Because those that put down $1 to reserve the product before a launch are 30x more likely to buy](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/how-to-build-a-massive-pre-campaign-email-list-without-spending-a-dime/)
.

Step 3: Scaling Our Best Assets With Proprietary Audiences
----------------------------------------------------------

[Through extensive testing on different ad creative and landing pages](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/how-to-test-your-ads-like-launchboom/)
, we ended up with the following best ad and landing page designs:

Ad:

![Author Clock Top Performing Facebook Ad](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/image-1.png)

Landing Page (Hero Section Pictured):

![Author Clock Landing Page Hero](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/image-2-1024x574.png)

Once we had tested out what was driving the most traffic and converting the most leads and reservations, we pressed on the gas by increasing our budget and testing out new audiences.

First, we found incredible performance when testing “Newspaper” and “Comic Book” interests. After that, we continued scaling by bringing in one of our most valuable advertising assets—**our proprietary crowdfunding backer lists**.

LaunchBoom has worked on hundreds of crowdfunding campaigns and has the email lists of millions of crowdfunding backers from those campaigns. Segmenting those users by product category and **creating lookalike audiences of them is an extremely powerful way to target high-quality users you can’t find just through Facebook’s normal interest targeting mechanics**.

_Lookalike audiences are audiences that Facebook creates by leveraging information like demographics, interests and behaviors from your existing customers to find new people who share similar qualities. When you use a lookalike audience, your ad is delivered to that audience of people who are similar to (or “look like”) your existing customers._

Step 4: Implementing Our Learnings Into a High-Performance Campaign Page
------------------------------------------------------------------------

The last step in making sure our campaign was set up for success was to build all of our learnings into a campaign page that would resonate with our list and convert the most backers.

First, we put our best-performing Landing Page Headline at the very top of the campaign page.

![Author Clock Campaign Page](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/image-3.png)

Then, we structured the rest of the page in order of what features got the best engagement from our leads.

Once we finally launched the campaign on October 12, 2021, we blasted the campaign link to our pre-campaign list and **generated a massive raise of $296,741 in just 24 hours**!

[Breaking six figures on your first day is a huge win](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/take-your-6-figure-campaign-to-7-figures/)
, and really helps to create tons of momentum and organic traffic from Kickstarter’s community when everyone on the site sees what a great start Author Clock is off to… and there’s still 29 days left!

Are you looking to launch a product soon? [Get in touch with us so we can learn more about you and your new product](https://www.launchboom.com/apply/)
!

![Lauchboom Logo](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/f-logo.svg "Lauchboom Logo")

# Meet the Crowdfunding Team: Creative Producers - LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy

[Menu](#)
 [](https://www.launchboom.com)
[Talk  \
To Us](/expert)

![LaunchBoom meet the team creative producers](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/02/Meet-the-Team-Creative-Producers-Feature-1024x576.jpg)

It’s hard to know what you’re getting when you decide to work with a marketing agency. Many advertise themselves as experts, but if you don’t know what you’re looking for, you could end up getting burned by an agency.

There are a lot of factors that qualify LaunchBoom as [one of the best in the business](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/what-crowdfunding-experts-have-learned-over-5000-campaigns/)
, like our expert certifications or our proven crowdfunding track record. But, nothing qualifies us better than the people working here who make it all happen each and every day.

From the producers in the studios to the data-crunching marketers, LaunchBoom is composed of several specialized teams who work together to turn clients’ aspirations of success into reality.

Today, we’re giving you an in-depth look into the LaunchBoom Creative Producers. They are experts at what they do, so I’ll allow them to elaborate on their roles directly!

Contents

*   [What is a Creative Producer?](#what-is-a-creative-producer)
    
*   [What is the CP’s role on each team?](#what-is-the-cps-role-on-each-team)
    
*   [What’s the most important part of production?](#whats-the-most-important-part-of-production)
    
*   [What’s your process for making great content?](#whats-your-process-for-making-great-content)
    
*   [What is the toughest hurdle you often encounter?](#what-is-the-toughest-hurdle-you-often-encounter)
    
*   [Fun Question Time!](#fun-question-time)
    

What is a Creative Producer?
----------------------------

![meet the team LaunchBoom creative producers](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/02/MTT-CP-1024x361.jpg)

**Reed:** A Creative Producer (CP) is the team member who conceptualizes and creates the photo and [video assets](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/your-crowdfunding-video-is-more-important-than-you-think/)
 for our clients’ ads, landing pages, and campaigns. Creative Producers hold an interesting position somewhere between marketers and artists. They are problem solvers and conceptualizers.

**Jayne:** Creative Producer roles can mean a lot of things throughout different industries and companies. For us, the Creative Producers handle things beyond project management. I like to think that we produce creative work and do literally a little bit of everything from timelines, to art direction, to shooting the physical product and final editing.

What is the CP’s role on each team?
-----------------------------------

**Reed:** On the Crowdfunding Team, CP’s ideate ads intended to stop the scroll and convert viewers to customers. We coordinate with the Campaign Strategists to review performance analytics and make changes before and during crowdfunding campaigns. Most of the time, the CP is responsible for casting, styling, scripting, executing, and editing the final assets.

**Jayne:** My role on the Scaleboom team is to really understand the client’s past and present metrics and creative. This means working closely with the managers of each client. [We have to understand current ad trends](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/top-5-facebook-ads-that-will-drive-traffic-to-your-ecommerce-site/)
 and audiences for those products. I brainstorm ideas with the managers and predict what would work for prospecting and retargeting. I then plan out timelines that work with the managers and deadlines, shoot the ads or web content, and edit. Throughout the editing phase, I then work closely with the managers again to receive feedback and reiterate to make it the best content possible.

What’s the most important part of production?
---------------------------------------------

![LaunchBoom meet the team creative producer Reed](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/02/Creative-Producer-Reed.jpg)

**Reed:** Pre-production. The time and energy that goes into a production before the shoot day makes the biggest difference. Spending time on the front end allows for more efficient shoot days which in turn makes for faster editing. There are frequent difficulties that come up in the middle of production that can be mitigated by spending more time on pre-production planning like lighting tests, location scouting, running through complicated camera movements, etc.

**Jayne:** The most important part of production is what comes before the actual production. [There is a lot of planning that goes into every shoot](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/behind-the-scenes-creating-the-shot-for-tibutton-launchboom-studios/)
, whether big or small. Understanding the product and its audience is key to everything we make. First we figure out what the audience wants/needs, and trends that they lean towards. Then we look into production details such as the model’s age/gender/ethnicity, props that will be in the image/video, words and tonality, and syntax that will be used in the video, location, and many other factors. These all come together to create the best content.

What’s your process for making great content?
---------------------------------------------

**Reed:** First, familiarizing myself with the client through research. Then, putting together a simple shot list with the basics that I know I’ll need to capture (studio photography, shots that simply highlight the main features, etc). And after the simple shot list is down I try and be as creative as possible with the remainder of my shot list. I look through competitors in the same industry to see what is trending and I also try very hard to pull inspiration from other, non-relevant brands and industries to see how I can bring a unique look to a product.

**Jayne:** I would say my process for making great content is mostly what happens in pre-production. This includes an introduction of the project, understanding the client’s company, branding, and product. After the team’s Greenlight meeting, I will go through and brainstorm with everyone and then [produce a creative treatment that highlights details of the company,](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/6-tips-for-a-six-figure-kickstarter-video-753d2a9c0090/)
 product, mood boards, idea outline, shot list, script, production details, and many more. During production day, we just got to execute it and create the best content possible with the edit in mind. During the editing phase, there will occasionally be lots of back and forth with feedback and iterations.

What is the toughest hurdle you often encounter?
------------------------------------------------

![LaunchBoom meet the team creative producer Jayne](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/02/Creative-Producer-Jayne.jpg)

**Reed:** Working with prototypes is very difficult. Often, they have limited functionality, are fragile, and are [the only ones in existence.](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/prepare-for-a-successful-crowdfunding-manufacturing-experience/)
 Trying to showcase the product in use when some of the main functions aren’t operable is when our creative problem-solving skills really come in handy. A popular feature of many products is their durability; this can be difficult to highlight when the prototype is a very expensive, 1-of-1, fragile, 3D printed model.

**Jayne:** The toughest hurdle I used to encounter was non-functional prototypes. Nowadays, it’s usually tough clients and very limited budgets. We are always trying to find creative solutions to create assets and content with limited resources and budget constraints. There definitely have been difficult challenges to find workarounds for, but it has been quite fun to problem solve.

Fun Question Time!
------------------

### What’s the most fun project you’ve worked on at LaunchBoom?

**Reed:** [Bubble Hotels](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/how-we-raised-690453-for-bubble-hotels-on-indiegogo-case-study/)
 and BodyPluv were the most fun campaigns for me. We put 100% of our team on those projects and I really enjoyed the collaborative opportunity that they provided. Working together on larger projects is really enjoyable for me and I think is the best way for me to grow as a creative.

**Jayne:** Oh my! There have been so many fun projects that I’ve done with LaunchBoom. I would have to say all projects that I got to work with my team on. Off the top of my head, Bubble Hotel and Bodyfly. It was a full LaunchBoom creative crew production, and that has always been the highlight. Bubble Hotel, we got to travel and create outside for a week as a team for the first time which has always been my goal as a creative. Bodyfly was another fun and smaller production that I got to work with everyone on the team that took place in our studio.

* * *

Ready to find out firsthand how our Creative Producers can help bring your branding ideas to life? [Book a call with us today!](https://www.launchboom.com/apply/)

Also, if you enjoyed reading about the Creative Producer role here at LaunchBoom, check out some of our other Meet the Team spotlights:

[Campaign Managers](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/meet-the-team-campaign-managers/)
                               [Campaign Strategists](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/meet-the-team-campaign-strategists/)
                                    [Copywriters](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/meet-the-team-copywriters/)

# LaunchBoom Learning: Timeline of a TestBoom - LaunchBoom - Indiegogo & Kickstarter Marketing Strategy

[Menu](#)
 [](https://www.launchboom.com)
[Talk  \
To Us](/expert)

![Timeline of a TestBoom feature image](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/02/Blog-Post-12.16.21-–-3-1024x576.jpg)

Crowdfunding is the best way to bring a consumer product to market because a successful campaign on Kickstarter or Indiegogo can pay for so many of your startup expenses. And though crowdfunding comes with its own set of risks, **there’s something you can do to mitigate them: testing.**

Testing a product’s viability gives you an idea of how it will perform during an actual crowdfunding launch. At LaunchBoom, we’ve developed our own system for testing products that we call TestBoom.

*   The value of a TestBoom can’t be overstated, because it tells you:
*   If there’s enough demand for your product to make a launch worth it
*   What specific copy, graphics, GIFs, and videos bring in the most potential customers at the lowest cost to you
*   What messaging resonates with your audience
*   How much of your email list is likely to convert
*   What the best price for your product is

[Discovering these learnings is important,](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/testing-your-crowdfunding-idea-will-save-you-money/)
 but so is knowing how we arrive at those results. Committing to a process like TestBoom can feel like a leap of faith, which is why we want to give you an inside look.

Here’s everything you need to know about the timeline of a TestBoom broken down into its key phases.

### Table of Contents

1.  [Phase 1: Onboarding](#phase1)
    
2.  [Phase 2: Kickoff and Messaging](#phase2)
    
3.  [Phase 3: Deliverables](#phase3)
    
4.  [Phase 4: Testing](#phase4)
    
5.  [Phase 5: Final Results](#phase5)
    

Contents

*   [Phase 1: Onboarding (2 Weeks)](#phase-1-onboarding-2-weeks)
    
*   [Phase 2: Kickoff and Messaging (1 Week)](#phase-2-kickoff-and-messaging-1-week)
    
*   [Phase 3: Deliverables (3 Weeks)](#phase-3-deliverables-3-weeks)
    
*   [Phase 4: Testing (3-4 Weeks)](#phase-4-testing-3-4-weeks)
    
*   [Phase 5: Final Results](#phase-5-final-results)
    

Phase 1: Onboarding (2 Weeks)
-----------------------------

Once you’ve signed up for TestBoom, we’ll provide you with an account and login to our onboarding app.

Think of the onboarding app like one giant checklist. We include every step you’ll need to take for us to start a TestBoom, the biggest of which is the Key Information Questionnaire. This is where you’ll provide us with everything we need to know about you, your company, and your product, so we can create the best product positioning possible within the crowdfunding space.

On top of that, there are also various administrative steps that you’ll go through like linking us with your Stripe account so we can receive reservation deposits from customers, and registering with Mailchimp for email marketing. We provide instructions and guides to make this as easy as possible and have onboarding specialists who can help you at any time if any areas are confusing. If you’ve got other existing assets like product photos, email lists, or a functional prototype, this is when you’d send them to us.

If you can’t provide any visuals that we can use for running ads and building landing pages, you can provide us with CAD models of the product so we can have professional 3D renders done by the time we need them for landing page development.

Here’s an example of a render we can create:

![Timeline of a TestBoom render photo](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/02/Cooler-Keg-TestBoom-Render-1024x640.jpg)

**Onboarding overall is a straightforward process, but it’s important to note that how quickly this phase gets completed relies mostly on you.** We’ve fine-tuned this process to make it as easy as possible, but you can complete it at your own pace.

Phase 2: Kickoff and Messaging (1 Week)
---------------------------------------

[Every new client is given a Campaign Manager](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/meet-the-team-campaign-managers/)
 (CM), who is the main point of contact between the creator and LaunchBoom’s Crowdfunding team. A Kickoff call is scheduled between you and your CM, and the TestBoom process can finally begin. This is where the CM will answer a lot of your questions and establish expectations.

**The other benefit to the Kickoff call is that you’ll be able to communicate your ideas about product messaging.** Nobody knows your product like you do, so we value all of your input. It allows us to strengthen our own approach to creative strategy.

After the Kickoff Call is done, your Campaign Manager will build out the project timeline and assign tasks to the team that will be working on your project.

The first step in our process is product research and positioning. Our copywriters will comb through your Key Information Questionnaire and compile all relevant information into a messaging summary. This summary will be the foundation of our strategy moving into the next phase.

Phase 3: Deliverables (3 Weeks)
-------------------------------

In this stage, the LaunchBoom team springs to life. The main goal here is to [deliver a professional landing page](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/5-tips-to-design-a-landing-page-for-crowdfunding-that-converts/)
 for your product where customers can reserve a spot for a crowdfunding launch. Utilizing the skills of the Campaign Strategists, Designers, Copywriters, and Developers, we’re able to put together some incredible content.

Example of landing page

Every landing page starts as a written document with headlines supported by body copy and design ideas. This is where we identify a product’s unique selling propositions (USPs) and figure out how to leverage them into high conversion rates.

From there, our graphic designers are tasked with creating the look of the page. All existing visual assets like photos, renders, and videos are important resources we can use to create an engaging landing page.

One important thing to note is that through each of the stages described above, we take your input into account. Each landing page goes through several rounds of internal feedback, but your opinion is just as valuable. **No deliverable will ever go live without getting your approval first.**

Once the design and the copy are ready, the development team will put it all together into a beautiful website. After that, we’re ready to start advertising!

Phase 4: Testing (3-4 Weeks)
----------------------------

From here, our Campaign Strategists are finally ready to start putting your ad spend to work. Using data that we’ve gathered across hundreds of campaigns, we’re able to create highly specific audiences to target on Facebook.

Each week, strategists run different variations of ads to test different metrics like headlines, copy, or images. When certain variations perform well, we can use them to optimize the landing page and ad strategy to achieve better Cost Per Reservations (CPRs). For a more in-depth look at how this funnel works, [check out this article.](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/how-to-build-a-lead-gen-funnel-for-kickstarter-or-indiegogo-that-converts/)

Every new result produces a new piece of the TestBoom puzzle. **Over the course of a month, we compile the data into ad reports that Campaign Managers share with you on a weekly basis.** We don’t want to keep you in the dark while we’re testing so we make sure you understand the thought processes behind each of our testing decisions.

Ultimately, we’re able to gather enough data to make a final decision on whether your product will find success within our system or not. That brings us to the final phase of the process.

Phase 5: Final Results
----------------------

Every TestBoom aims to determine a product’s viability–specifically the viability to move forward into a full crowdfunding launch with our agency. Full launches are a heavy investment from both our clients and our team, and it’s our responsibility to determine if it’s going to be a worthwhile investment for both of us.

### Full Launch

If the metrics indicate that your product is scalable within our system and that we’re going to have a successful launch together, it’s time to ramp up! We’ll go over all of the learnings together to get aligned on the strategy moving forward, and then start pouring on the gas.

### Other Options

If the data doesn’t support moving forward with a launch, we enter the final phase of the process. Campaign Managers will host a Wrap-Up call with you to give a general overview of the testing, what we learned, and how you can use it moving forward.

Typically, when TestBoom’s don’t indicate we’ll be able to get you a strong enough Cost per Acquisition to scale, then it’s best not to move into a full launch where you’ll have to invest significantly more money into ad spend and creative production.

However, we still have many resources and connections to provide you with to make sure you can still launch your crowdfunding campaign. Maybe LaunchBoom Consulting will be a more affordable option for you where they can assist you on your launch every step of the way. Perhaps your product is [already a good fit for eCommerce](https://www.launchboom.com/blog/how-to-transition-from-crowdfunding-to-ecommerce-in-2022/)
 so we can connect you with our ScaleBoom team.

Launching a product with crowdfunding can be confusing, and we’re here to make sure that in the end, you have the resources you need along with the invaluable data you’ll gain from your TestBoom.

I hope this TestBoom breakdown helped you understand our process a little better here at LaunchBoom. If you feel like your product is ready for a TestBoom, or just want to find out more information about our agency, [get in touch with us anytime.](https://www.launchboom.com/apply/)

![Lauchboom Logo](https://www.launchboom.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/f-logo.svg "Lauchboom Logo")
